	desc = hallfredhavn.4.d
	picture = FAMINE_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	major_trigger = {
		has_discovered = AD5
	}

	option = {
		name = hallfredhavn.4.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
#		every_owned_province = {
#			remove_country_modifier = AD5_skraeling_slavery
#			remove_country_modifier = AD5_mediocre_seeds
#		}
		set_global_flag = ACE_hallfred_ruins_flag
		custom_tooltip = AD5_ceases_to_exist_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			disband_all_ships = yes
			remove_country = yes
		}
		2302 = {
			add_permanent_province_modifier = {
				name = AD5_gerudian_ruins_modifier
				duration = -1
			}
			change_native_size = 20
			change_native_ferocity = 10
			change_native_hostileness = 5
		}
		2304 = {
			add_permanent_province_modifier = {
				name = AD5_gerudian_runestones
				duration = -1
			}
			change_native_size = 5
			change_native_ferocity = 10
			change_native_hostileness = 5
		}
		2301 = {
			change_native_size = 10
			change_native_ferocity = 10
			change_native_hostileness = 5
		}
		6559 = { add_human_minority_size_effect = yes }
	}
}

#Gerudian Ruins on the Dry Coast
country_event = {
	id = hallfredhavn.5
	title = hallfredhavn.5.t
	desc = hallfredhavn.5.d
	picture = RUNESTONE_eventPicture
	goto = 2302
	
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = no
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = ACE_hallfred_ruins_flag
		NOT = { has_country_flag = ACE_discovered_hallfred_ruins_flag }
		has_discovered = 2302
		has_discovered = 2304
		capital_scope = { continent = europe }
		OR = {
			num_of_explorers = 1
			num_of_conquistadors = 1
			primary_culture = pearlsedger
			tag = A11
			culture_group = gerudian
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = ACE_discovered_hallfred_ruins_flag
		}
	}

	option = { #huh neat
		name = hallfredhavn.5.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}

	option = { #huh neat
		name = hallfredhavn.5.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		highlight = yes
		trigger = {
			culture_group = gerudian
		}
		add_prestige = 10
	}

	option = { #
		name = hallfredhavn.5.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		highlight = yes
		trigger = {
			or = {
				primary_culture = pearlsedger
				tag = A11
			}
		}
		add_prestige = 25
	}
}

#Gudafridr event
country_event = {
	id = hallfredhavn.7
	title = hallfredhavn.7.t
	desc = hallfredhavn.7.d
	picture = DIPLOMACY_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #restore gudafridr
		name = hallfredhavn.7.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		remove_estate_privilege = estate_church_AD5_broken_gudafridr
		set_estate_privilege = estate_church_AD5_gudafridr_proclamation
		add_treasury = -50
		add_stability = 1
	}
	option = { #skaldhyrric nation
		trigger = {
			religion = skaldhyrric_faith
		}
		name = hallfredhavn.7.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		highlight = yes
		remove_estate_privilege = estate_church_AD5_broken_gudafridr
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = AD5_religious_consolidation
			duration = 3650
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					religion = skaldhyrric_faith
				}
			}
			add_unrest = 10
		}
	}

	option = { #Cannorian nation
		trigger = {
			religion = cannorian_pantheon
		}
		name = hallfredhavn.7.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		highlight = yes
		remove_estate_privilege = estate_church_AD5_broken_gudafridr
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = AD5_religious_consolidation
			duration = 3650
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					religion = cannorian_pantheon
				}
			}
			add_unrest = 10
		}
	}
}

#Stadfastr yearly commands
country_event = {
	id = hallfredhavn.10
	title = hallfredhavn.10.t
	desc = hallfredhavn.10.d
	picture = DIPLOMACY_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			mission_completed = AD5_end_the_sidrvetr
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = hallfredhavn.10
				days = 365
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #focus on fishing
		name = hallfredhavn.10.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				mission_completed = AD5_end_the_sidrvetr
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = ACE_ad5_cant_use_ship_next_year_flag
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = AD5_stadfastr_fishing_flag
		add_treasury = -25
		country_event_with_effect_insight = {
			id = hallfredhavn.11
			days = 334
			effect = "
				hallfredhavn_fishing_effect = yes
			"
		}
	}

	option = { #focus on trading valuables for food
		name = hallfredhavn.10.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				mission_completed = AD5_end_the_sidrvetr
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = ACE_ad5_cant_use_ship_next_year_flag
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = AD5_stadfastr_food_trading_flag
		add_treasury = -25
		country_event_with_effect_insight = {
			id = hallfredhavn.12
			days = 334
			effect = "
				hallfredhavn_food_purchase_effect = yes
			"
		}
	}

	option = { #raid the Skegglanders (Taychend)
		name = hallfredhavn.10.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = ACE_ad5_cant_use_ship_next_year_flag
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = AD5_stadfastr_raiding_flag
		add_treasury = -25
		country_event_with_effect_insight = {
			id = hallfredhavn.13
			days = 334
			effect = "
				hallfredhavn_raid_effect = yes
			"
		}
	}

	option = { #trade with the Skegglanders (Taychend)
		name = hallfredhavn.10.e
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = ACE_ad5_cant_use_ship_next_year_flag
			}
		}

		add_treasury = -25

			id = hallfredhavn.14
			days = 334
			effect = "
				hallfredhavn_trade_effect = yes
			"
		}
	}

#Landsnámsverk Event
country_event = {
	id = hallfredhavn.39
	title = hallfredhavn.39.t
	desc = hallfredhavn.39.d
	picture = COLONIZATION_eventPicture
	goto = event_province
	
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_colony = yes
				}
				save_event_target_as = event_province
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #go back
		name = hallfredhavn.39.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		#highlight = yes
		clr_country_flag = AD5_landsnamsverk_interface_open_flag
	}

	option = { #Use manpower
		name = hallfredhavn.39.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		goto = event_province
		trigger = {
			manpower = 0.2
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = AD5_landsnamsverk_manpower_modifier }
		}
		add_manpower = -0.2
		add_treasury = -10
		event_target:event_province = {
			add_colonysize = 100
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = AD5_landsnamsverk_manpower_modifier
			duration = 365
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = AD5_landsnamsverk_sailors_modifier }
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = AD5_landsnamsverk_manpower_modifier }
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = AD5_landsnamsverk_forced_emigration_modifier }
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = hallfredhavn.137
				}
			}
			else = {
				clr_country_flag = AD5_landsnamsverk_interface_open_flag
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Use sailors
		name = hallfredhavn.39.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		goto = event_province
		trigger = {
			sailors = 200
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = AD5_landsnamsverk_sailors_modifier }
		}
		add_sailors = -200
		add_treasury = -10
		event_target:event_province = {
			add_colonysize = 100
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = AD5_landsnamsverk_sailors_modifier
			duration = 365
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = AD5_landsnamsverk_sailors_modifier }
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = AD5_landsnamsverk_manpower_modifier }
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = AD5_landsnamsverk_forced_emigration_modifier }
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = hallfredhavn.137
				}
			}
			else = {
				clr_country_flag = AD5_landsnamsverk_interface_open_flag
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Force Emigration
		name = hallfredhavn.39.e
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			2302 = {
				base_tax = 2
				base_production = 2
				base_manpower = 2
			}
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = AD5_landsnamsverk_forced_emigration_modifier }
		}
		2302 = {
			random_list = {
				33 = { add_base_tax = -1 }
				33 = { add_base_production = -1 }
				33 = { add_base_manpower = -1 }
			}
			add_unrest = 2
		}
		add_treasury = -10
		event_target:event_province = {
			add_colonysize = 500
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = AD5_landsnamsverk_forced_emigration_modifier
			duration = 730
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = AD5_landsnamsverk_sailors_modifier }
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = AD5_landsnamsverk_manpower_modifier }
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = AD5_landsnamsverk_forced_emigration_modifier }
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = hallfredhavn.137
				}
			}
			else = {
				clr_country_flag = AD5_landsnamsverk_interface_open_flag
			}
		}
	}
}

		inherit = J79

	desc = hallfredhavn.41.d

	goto = 6503
	
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Fish
		name = hallfredhavn.41.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		6503 = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = AD5_aquatic_industry_focus
				duration = 18250
			}
			add_base_production = 2
			change_trade_goods = fish
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_port = yes
				trade_goods = fish
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = AD5_aquatic_industry_focus
				duration = 18250
			}
			add_base_production = 2
		}
	}

		}

	}

#Reformation of the Thing
country_event = {
	id = hallfredhavn.43
	title = hallfredhavn.43.t
	desc = hallfredhavn.43.d
	picture = DEBATE_REPUBLICAN_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #"Law and Order will be paramount in the coming years."
		name = hallfredhavn.43.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		add_government_reform = egalitarian_thing_reform
		add_government_reform = republican_authoritarianism_reform
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = AD5_law_and_order_modifier
			duration = 3650
		}
		custom_tooltip = AD5_new_runestone_tt
	}

	option = { #"The descendants of the Fyrstýrimenn deserve to have their voices heard."
		name = hallfredhavn.43.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		add_government_reform = egalitarian_thing_reform
		add_government_reform = nepotism_reform
		add_stability_or_adm_power = yes
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_nobles
			loyalty = 10
		}
		custom_tooltip = AD5_new_runestone_tt
	}

	option = { #"We have to enshrine new traditions."
		name = hallfredhavn.43.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		add_government_reform = egalitarian_thing_reform
		add_government_reform = republicanism_reform
		add_republican_tradition = 10
		custom_tooltip = AD5_new_runestone_tt
	}

	option = { #"We have to strengthen the Meritocracy."
		name = hallfredhavn.43.e
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		add_government_reform = egalitarian_thing_reform
		add_government_reform = democratic_values_reform
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = AD5_meritocracy_modifier
			duration = 3650
		}
		custom_tooltip = AD5_new_runestone_tt
	}

	option = { #"We have to protect the Nobility from the commoners almost as much as we must protect the commoners from the Nobility."
		name = hallfredhavn.43.f
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		add_government_reform = egalitarian_thing_reform
		add_government_reform = aristocratic_values_reform
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_nobles
			loyalty = 20
		}
		custom_tooltip = AD5_new_runestone_tt
	}

	option = { #"We cannot forget our religious values."
		name = hallfredhavn.43.g
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_estate_privilege = estate_church_AD5_gudafridr_proclamation
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		add_government_reform = egalitarian_thing_reform
		add_government_reform = religious_values_reform
		define_advisor = {
			type = inquisitor
			skill = 2
			discount = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = AD5_new_runestone_tt
	}
}

				colonysize = 300
				owned_by = AD5
			}

				owned_by = AD5
			}
		}
	}

		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		2300 = {
			change_trade_goods = iron
			add_colonysize = 100
		}
	}
}

#Revolving Jarldom Diceroll Event
country_event = {
	id = hallfredhavn.49
	title = hallfredhavn.49.t
	desc = hallfredhavn.49.d
	picture = DEBATE_REPUBLICAN_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_reform = revolving_jarldom_reform
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = ACE_revolving_jarldom_election_in_effect_flag
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = AD5_just_elected_a_ruler 
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = ACE_revolving_jarldom_election_in_effect_flag
			define_ruler = {
				name = "(Stadhafi)"
				adm = 2
				dip = 2
				mil = 2
				regency = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #"Roll the dice"
		name = hallfredhavn.49.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		random_list = {
			16 = { #A Svartskegg Jarl!
				country_event = {
					id = hallfredhavn.50
				}
			}
			83 = { #A Divenscourge Jarl!
				country_event = {
					id = hallfredhavn.51
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#A Svartskegg Jarl
country_event = {
	id = hallfredhavn.50
	title = hallfredhavn.50.t
	desc = hallfredhavn.50.d
	picture = 3_SONS_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_reform = revolving_jarldom_reform
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				33 = {
					set_country_flag = harem_fairest_heir #Completely Random
				}
				33 = {
					set_country_flag = harem_strong_heir #Atleast 1 MIl
				}
				33 = {
					set_country_flag = harem_leadership_heir #Atleast 1 MIL
				}
				1 = {
					set_country_flag = harem_genious_heir #Atleast 1 in every stat.
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				33 = {
					set_country_flag = harem_studious_heir #Atleast 1 ADM
				}
				33 = {
					set_country_flag = harem_pious_heir #Atleast 1 ADM
				}
				33 = {
					set_country_flag = harem_inquisitive_heir #Completely Random
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				33 = {
					set_country_flag = harem_gregarious_heir #Atleast 1 DIP
				}
				33 = {
					set_country_flag = harem_entrepreneurial_heir #Atleast 1 DIP
				}
				33 = {
					set_country_flag = harem_generous_heir #Completely Random
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = harem_events.1.a #Pious
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			has_country_flag = harem_pious_heir
		}
		define_ruler = {
			dynasty = Svartrskegg
			religion = skaldhyrric_faith
			male = yes
			change_adm = 1
			max_random_dip = 5
		}
	}
	option = {	 
		name = harem_events.1.b #Strong
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			has_country_flag = harem_strong_heir
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = tur_weakened_the_harem }
			define_ruler = {
				dynasty = Svartrskegg
				religion = skaldhyrric_faith
				male = yes
				change_mil = 1
				max_random_dip = 3
			}
		}
		else = {
			define_ruler = {
				dynasty = Svartrskegg
				religion = skaldhyrric_faith
				male = yes
				change_mil = 1
				max_random_dip = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	 
		name = harem_events.1.c #Studious
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			has_country_flag = harem_studious_heir
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = tur_weakened_the_harem }
			define_ruler = {
				dynasty = Svartrskegg
				religion = skaldhyrric_faith
				male = yes
				change_adm = 1
				max_random_mil = 3
			}
		}
		else = {
			define_ruler = {
				dynasty = Svartrskegg
				religion = skaldhyrric_faith
				male = yes
				change_adm = 1
				max_random_mil = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	 
		name = harem_events.1.e #leadership
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			has_country_flag = harem_leadership_heir
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = tur_weakened_the_harem }
			define_ruler = {
				dynasty = Svartrskegg
				religion = skaldhyrric_faith
				male = yes
				change_mil = 1
				max_random_adm = 3
			}
		}
		else = {
			define_ruler = {
				dynasty = Svartrskegg
				religion = skaldhyrric_faith
				male = yes
				change_mil = 1
				max_random_adm = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	 
		name = harem_events.1.d

#Vidarvotar slave efficiency adding
country_event = {
	id = hallfredhavn.54
	title = hallfredhavn.54.t
	desc = hallfredhavn.54.d
	picture = INVASION_ALLIES_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = no
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		has_faction = ad5_faction_vidarfotar
		faction_in_power = ad5_faction_vidarfotar
		any_owned_province = {
			trade_goods = slaves
			NOT = {
				has_province_modifier = AD5_vidarfotar_influence
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #
		name = hallfredhavn.54.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				trade_goods = slaves
				NOT = {
					has_province_modifier = AD5_vidarfotar_influence
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = AD5_vidarfotar_influence
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

		}

		tag = AD5
	}

		days = 1000
	}

	option = { #It is their ship after all
		name = hallfredhavn.57.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		custom_tooltip = ACE_ad5_cant_use_ship_next_year_tt
		set_country_flag = ACE_ad5_cant_use_ship_next_year_flag
		change_variable = {
			which = variable_AD5_hallfredhavn_trades
			value = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				6559 = {
					owned_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			6559 = {
				add_permanent_province_modifier = {
					name = AD5_small_skali_trading_outpost_modifier
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			6559 = {
				owner = {
					country_event = {
						id = hallfredhavn.58
						days = 365
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Overruled!
		name = hallfredhavn.57.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		add_faction_influence = {
			faction = ad5_faction_skalir
			influence = -1
		}
	}
}

	desc = hallfredhavn.60.d

	is_triggered_only = no

		tag = AD5

			rebel_type = slavery_abolitionists_rebels
			value = 80
		}
		NOT = {
			mission_completed = AD5_end_the_sidrvetr
		}
	}

	option = { #We cannot arrest people on rumors alone.
		name = hallfredhavn.60.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		custom_tooltip = AD5_abolitionists_tt
		spawn_rebels = {
			type = slavery_abolitionists_rebels
			size = 2
			leader = "Lilian Pearlsguard"
		}
	}

	option = { #Damn the laws, arrest them all!
		name = hallfredhavn.60.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		custom_tooltip = AD5_no_abolitionists_tt
		add_faction_influence = {
			faction = ad5_faction_pearlsguarders
			influence = -10
		}
		add_faction_influence = {
			faction = ad5_faction_vidarfotar
			influence = 10
		}
		random = {
			chance = 50
			spawn_rebels = {
				type = slavery_abolitionists_rebels
				size = 1
				leader = "Lilian Pearlsguard"
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #orwaiiification
	id = hallfredhavn.65
	title = hallfredhavn.65.t
	desc = hallfredhavn.65.d
	picture = INVASION_ALLIES_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = no
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = AD5_orwaiiification_flag
		any_owned_province = {
			religion_group = effelai
			NOT = {
				religion = orwaii
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 120
	}

	option = { #Let them do what they do best
		name = hallfredhavn.65.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = effelai
				NOT = {
					religion = orwaii
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					culture_group = degenerated_elf
				}
				change_culture = hallfreder
				change_religion = ROOT
			}
			else = {
				change_culture = oonoi
				change_religion = orwaii
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = hallfredhavn.73
	title = hallfredhavn.73.t
	desc = hallfredhavn.73.d
	picture = BAD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = AD5_is_or_was_hallfredhavn_flag
		OR = {
			has_reform = stratified_thing_reform
			has_reform = egalitarian_thing_reform
		}
		NOT = {
			has_ruler_modifier = AD5_stubborn_ruler
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				faction_in_power = ad5_faction_divenscourges
				NOT = {
					has_ruler_modifier = ACE_hallfredhavn_ruler_divenscourge
				}
			}
			AND = {
				faction_in_power = ad5_faction_pearlsguarders
				NOT = {
					has_ruler_modifier = ACE_hallfredhavn_ruler_pearlsguard
				}
			}
			AND = {
				faction_in_power = ad5_faction_svartskeggs
				NOT = {
					has_ruler_modifier = ACE_hallfredhavn_ruler_svartrskegg
				}
			}
			AND = {
				faction_in_power = ad5_faction_skalir
				NOT = {
					has_ruler_modifier = ACE_hallfredhavn_ruler_skali
				}
			}
			AND = {
				faction_in_power = ad5_faction_vidarfotar
				NOT = {
					has_ruler_modifier = ACE_hallfredhavn_ruler_vidarfotr
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 365
	}

	option = { #accept change
		name = hallfredhavn.73.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		hidden_effect = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = AD5_just_elected_a_ruler
				duration = 2
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_reform = stratified_thing_reform
			}
			add_government_power = {
				mechanic_type = anb_ace_egalitarians_vs_monarchists_mechanic
				power_type = governmental_power
				value = -5
			}
		}
		add_republican_tradition = 5
		if = {
			limit = {
				faction_in_power = ad5_faction_divenscourges
			}
			define_ruler = {
				dynasty = "Divenscourge"
			}
			add_ruler_modifier = {
				name = ACE_hallfredhavn_ruler_divenscourge
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				faction_in_power = ad5_faction_pearlsguarders
			}
			define_ruler = {
				dynasty = "Pearlsguard"
				religion = cannorian_pantheon
			}
			add_ruler_modifier = {
				name = ACE_hallfredhavn_ruler_pearlsguard
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				faction_in_power = ad5_faction_svartskeggs
			}
			define_ruler = {
				dynasty = "Svartrskegg"
				religion = skaldhyrric_faith
			}
			add_ruler_modifier = {
				name = ACE_hallfredhavn_ruler_svartrskegg
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				faction_in_power = ad5_faction_skalir
				NOT = {
					mission_completed = AD7_integrate_the_kynn
				}
			}
			define_ruler = {
				dynasty = "Skali"
			}
			add_ruler_modifier = {
				name = ACE_hallfredhavn_ruler_skali
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				faction_in_power = ad5_faction_skalir
				mission_completed = AD7_integrate_the_kynn
			}
			define_ruler = {
				dynasty = "Skali"
				culture = halfkynn_half_elf
			}
			add_ruler_modifier = {
				name = ACE_hallfredhavn_ruler_skali
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				faction_in_power = ad5_faction_vidarfotar
			}
			define_ruler = {
				dynasty = "Vidarfótr"
			}
			add_ruler_modifier = {
				name = ACE_hallfredhavn_ruler_vidarfotr
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #refuse change
		name = hallfredhavn.73.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		add_republican_tradition = -5
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_reform = stratified_thing_reform
			}
			add_government_power = {

			}
		}
		add_ruler_modifier = {
			name = AD5_stubborn_ruler
			duration = -1
		}
		add_stability = -1
	}

country_event = { #anti-slavery protests #todo
	id = hallfredhavn.75
	title = hallfredhavn.75.t
	desc = hallfredhavn.75.d
	picture = ANGRY_MOB_eventPicture
	goto = 2301
	
	is_triggered_only = no
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = AD5
		rebel_progress_at_least = {
			rebel_type = slavery_abolitionists_rebels
			value = 50
		}
		NOT = {
			mission_completed = AD5_end_the_sidrvetr
		}
	}

	option = { #LIBERTY OR DEATH
		name = hallfredhavn.75.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			has_ruler_modifier = ACE_hallfredhavn_ruler_pearlsguard
		}
		highlight = yes
		2301 = {
			spawn_rebels = {
				type = slavery_abolitionists_rebels
				size = 2
				leader = "Lilian Pearlsguard"
			}
		}
		add_faction_influence = {
			faction = ad5_faction_pearlsguarders
			influence = 10
		}
	}

	option = { #GO BACK TO WORK YOU SKRAELINGS
		name = hallfredhavn.75.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			has_ruler_modifier = ACE_hallfredhavn_ruler_vidarfotr
		}
		highlight = yes
		2301 = {
			hallfredhavn_expand_slavery = yes
			add_base_production = 1
			add_unrest = 10
		}
	}

	option = { #tank it
		name = hallfredhavn.75.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		2301 = {
			spawn_rebels = {
				type = slavery_abolitionists_rebels
				size = 1
				leader = "Lilian Pearlsguard"
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #
		name = hallfredhavn.75.e
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			mil_power = 100
		}
		highlight = yes
		add_mil_power = -100
		random = {
			chance = 50
			2301 = {
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = slavery_abolitionists_rebels
					size = 1
					leader = "Lilian Pearlsguard"
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Conversion of Province
	id = hallfredhavn.81
	title = hallfredhavn.81.t
	desc = hallfredhavn.81.d
	picture = RELIGIOUS_CONVERSION_eventPicture
	goto = event_province
	
	is_triggered_only = no
	fire_only_once = no
	hidden = no

	trigger = {
		tag = AD7
		mission_completed = AD5_pe3
		has_estate_privilege = estate_church_AD5_gudafridr_proclamation
		any_owned_province = {
			superregion = taychend_superregion
			NOT = {
				religion = cannorian_pantheon
			}
			has_tax_building_trigger = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_owned_province = {
						superregion = taychend_superregion
						NOT = {
							religion = cannorian_pantheon
						}
						has_building = cathedral
					}
				}
				random_province = {
					limit = {
						superregion = taychend_superregion
						NOT = {
							religion = cannorian_pantheon
						}
						has_building = cathedral
					}
					save_event_target_as = event_province
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_province = {
					limit = {
						superregion = taychend_superregion
						NOT = {
							religion = cannorian_pantheon
						}
						has_tax_building_trigger = yes
					}
					save_event_target_as = event_province
					set_province_flag = AD5_event_province_flag
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 36
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			any_owned_province = {
				superregion = taychend_superregion
				NOT = {
					religion = cannorian_pantheon
				}
				has_building = cathedral
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			employed_advisor = {
				type = inquisitor
				religion = cannorian_pantheon
				skill = 1
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			employed_advisor = {
				type = inquisitor
				religion = cannorian_pantheon
				skill = 2
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			employed_advisor = {
				type = inquisitor
				religion = cannorian_pantheon
				skill = 3
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #now they can focus on a neighbouring province
		name = hallfredhavn.81.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			event_target:event_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owned_by = ROOT
					NOT = {
						religion = cannorian_pantheon
					}
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:event_province = {
			change_religion = cannorian_pantheon
		}
		event_target:event_province = {
			random_neighbor_province = {
				limit = {
					owned_by = ROOT
					NOT = {
						religion = cannorian_pantheon
					}
				}
				random = {
					chance = 33
					change_religion = cannorian_pantheon
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #draft them into the army
		name = hallfredhavn.81.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		event_target:event_province = {
			change_religion = cannorian_pantheon
		}
		add_owned_provinces_development_manpower = {
			multiplier = 0.2
			age_multiplier = 1
			custom_tooltip = AD5_temple_manpower_tt
			trigger = {
				has_province_flag = AD5_event_province_flag
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #let them serve in the temple
		name = hallfredhavn.81.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		event_target:event_province = {
			change_religion = cannorian_pantheon
	#		add_base_tax = 1
			add_base_production = 1
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = AD5_event_province_flag
				}
				clr_province_flag = AD5_event_province_flag
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Settling of the Jötundalr
	id = hallfredhavn.82
	title = hallfredhavn.82.t
	desc = hallfredhavn.82.d
	picture = RELIGIOUS_CONVERSION_eventPicture
	goto = 2508
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = no

	option = { #
		name = hallfredhavn.82.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		custom_tooltip = AD5_jotundalr_settlements_tt
		tooltip = {
			capital_scope = {
				add_permanent_province_modifier = {
					name = AD5_jotundalr_settlements
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_province = {
				limit = {
					region = kalavend_region
				}
				add_human_minority_size_effect = yes
				add_permanent_province_modifier = {
					name = AD5_jotundalr_settlements
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				add_half_orcish_minority_size_effect = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = ACE_raided_harimari_flag
			}
			event_target:event_target_random = {
				add_harimari_minority_size_effect = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = ACE_raided_harpy_flag
			}
			event_target:event_target_random = {
				add_harpy_minority_size_effect = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = ACE_raided_hobgoblin_flag
			}
			event_target:event_target_random = {
				add_hobgoblin_minority_size_effect = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = ACE_raided_kobold_flag
			}
			event_target:event_target_random = {
				add_kobold_minority_size_effect = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = ACE_raided_lizardfolk_flag
			}
			event_target:event_target_random = {
				add_lizardfolk_minority_size_effect = yes
			}
		}
		if = {

				has_country_flag = ACE_raided_mechanim_flag
			}
			event_target:event_target_random = {
				add_mechanim_minority_size_effect = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = ACE_raided_ogre_flag
			}
			event_target:event_target_random = {
				add_ogre_minority_size_effect = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = ACE_raided_orcish_flag
			}
			event_target:event_target_random = {
				add_orcish_minority_size_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		clear_global_event_target = ACE_raid_target_event_target
		clr_country_flag = ACE_raided_ruinborn_flag
		clr_country_flag = ACE_raided_human_flag

		clr_country_flag = ACE_raided_centaur_flag
		clr_country_flag = ACE_raided_dwarven_flag

		clr_country_flag = ACE_raided_half_orcish_flag

#Republican tradition drops below 40
country_event = {
	id = hallfredhavn.87
	title = hallfredhavn.87.t
	desc = hallfredhavn.87.d
	picture = LIBERUM_VETO_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = no
	trigger = {
		has_reform = stratified_thing_reform
		NOT = {
			republican_tradition = 40
		}
	}

	option = { #invest in the government
		name = hallfredhavn.87.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		add_adm_power = -100
		add_treasury = -25
		add_republican_tradition = 5
	}

	option = { #let it burn
		name = hallfredhavn.87.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		add_government_power = {
			mechanic_type = anb_ace_egalitarians_vs_monarchists_mechanic
			power_type = governmental_power
			value = 10
		}
	}
}

#Militarisation following blooming
country_event = {
	id = hallfredhavn.91
	title = hallfredhavn.91.t
	desc = hallfredhavn.91.d
	picture = EFFELAI_BLOOM_ANIMATED_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #total war
		name = hallfredhavn.91.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					national_focus = MIL
				}
			}
			change_national_focus = MIL
		}
		unlock_merc_company = {
			merc_company = merc_rootburners
			free_merc = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = AD5_does_not_contr_fl_tt
		add_army_professionalism = 0.1
		add_army_tradition = 10
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = AD5_total_war
			duration = -1
		}
	}

	option = { #partial militarization
		name = hallfredhavn.91.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		unlock_merc_company = {
			merc_company = merc_rootburners
			free_merc = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = AD5_does_not_contr_fl_tt
		add_army_professionalism = 0.05
		add_army_tradition = 5
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = AD5_partial_militarisation
			duration = -1
		}
	}

	option = { #we'll be fine
		name = hallfredhavn.91.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		unlock_merc_company = {
			merc_company = merc_rootburners
			free_merc = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = AD5_does_not_contr_fl_tt
	}
}

#Armringr oath event
country_event = {

	desc = hallfredhavn.94.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = no

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {

				limit = {
					has_country_flag = event_target_armringr_flag
				}
				save_event_target_as = event_target_armringr

			}

country_event = {

	title = hallfredhavn.97.t
	desc = hallfredhavn.97.d
	picture = COURT_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = no

	major = yes
	major_trigger = {
		capital_scope = {
			OR = {
				continent = europe
				continent = south_america
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #pact of historical friendship
		name = hallfredhavn.97.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		custom_tooltip = AD5_historical_friendship_offer_tt
		A11 = {
			country_event = {
				id = hallfredhavn.105
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #try to pull migrants
		name = hallfredhavn.97.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = ACE_munas_forbidden_flag
			}
			custom_tooltip = ACE_new_deities_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_country_flag = ACE_munas_forbidden_flag
				clr_country_flag = ACE_nathalyne_forbidden_flag
				clr_country_flag = ACE_begga_forbidden_flag
				clr_country_flag = ACE_corin_forbidden_flag
			}
		}
		A11 = {
			add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = AD5_pulling_migrants
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = AD5_growing_human_minorities_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					superregion = taychend_superregion
					NOT = {
						culture_group = gerudian
						culture = halfkynn_half_elf
					}
				}
				add_human_minority_size_effect = yes
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					superregion = taychend_superregion
					NOT = {
						culture_group = gerudian
						culture = halfkynn_half_elf
					}
				}
				add_human_minority_size_effect = yes
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					superregion = taychend_superregion
					NOT = {
						culture_group = gerudian
						culture = halfkynn_half_elf
					}
				}
				add_human_minority_size_effect = yes
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					superregion = taychend_superregion
					NOT = {
						culture_group = gerudian

				id = hallfredhavn.115
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #try to pull migrants
		name = hallfredhavn.102.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		Z08 = {
			add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = AD5_pulling_migrants
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = AD5_growing_human_minorities_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					superregion = taychend_superregion
					NOT = {
						culture_group = gerudian
						culture = halfkynn_half_elf
					}
				}
				add_human_minority_size_effect = yes
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					superregion = taychend_superregion
					NOT = {
						culture_group = gerudian
						culture = halfkynn_half_elf
					}
				}
				add_human_minority_size_effect = yes
			}
			random_owned_province = {

					NOT = {

						culture = halfkynn_half_elf
					}
				}
				add_human_minority_size_effect = yes
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {

					NOT = {
						culture_group = gerudian
						culture = halfkynn_half_elf
					}
				}
				add_human_minority_size_effect = yes
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					superregion = taychend_superregion
					NOT = {
						culture_group = gerudian
						culture = halfkynn_half_elf
					}
				}
				add_human_minority_size_effect = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					area = nanru_nakar_area
				}
				NOT = {
					culture_group = gerudian
				}
				NOT = {
					has_province_flag = AD5_migration_target
				}
			}
			change_culture = east_dalr
			change_religion = skaldhyrric_faith
			add_base_tax = 2
			add_base_production = 2
			add_base_tax = 2
			set_province_flag = AD5_migration_target
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					area = nanru_nakar_area
				}
				NOT = {
					culture_group = gerudian
				}
				NOT = {

				}
			}
			change_culture = east_dalr

			add_base_tax = 2
			add_base_production = 2
			add_base_tax = 2
			set_province_flag = AD5_migration_target
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					area = nanru_nakar_area
				}
				NOT = {
					culture_group = gerudian
				}
				NOT = {

				}

	option = { #claim their aelantiri holdings
		name = hallfredhavn.102.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				alliance_with = Z08
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		every_province = {

					continent = north_america

	is_triggered_only = yes

			culture = halfkynn_half_elf

		}

#Halfkynn culture trait adder/remover
country_event = {
	id = hallfredhavn.119
	title = hallfredhavn.119.t
	desc = hallfredhavn.119.d
	picture = COURT_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = no
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		mission_completed = AD7_halfkynn_cultural_traits
		OR = {
			any_owned_province = {
				culture = halfkynn_half_elf
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = AD5_halfkynn_war_modifier
						has_province_modifier = AD5_halfkynn_trade_modifier
					}
				}
			}
			any_owned_province = {
				NOT = { culture = halfkynn_half_elf }
				OR = {
					has_province_modifier = AD5_halfkynn_war_modifier
					has_province_modifier = AD5_halfkynn_trade_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #accept
		name = hallfredhavn.119.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = AD5_halfkynn_trade_flag
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					culture = halfkynn_half_elf
					NOT = {
						has_province_modifier = AD5_halfkynn_trade_modifier
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = AD5_halfkynn_trade_modifier
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { culture = halfkynn_half_elf }
					has_province_modifier = AD5_halfkynn_trade_modifier
				}
				remove_province_modifier = AD5_halfkynn_trade_modifier
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = AD5_halfkynn_war_flag
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					culture = halfkynn_half_elf
					NOT = {
						has_province_modifier = AD5_halfkynn_war_modifier
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = AD5_halfkynn_war_modifier
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { culture = halfkynn_half_elf }
					has_province_modifier = AD5_halfkynn_war_modifier
				}
				remove_province_modifier = AD5_halfkynn_war_modifier
			}
		}
	}
}

	picture = NATIVES_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = no
	hidden = no

	trigger = {
		mission_completed = AD5_fate_of_the_oonoi
		any_owned_province = {
			any_empty_neighbor_province = {
				culture = oonoi
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			check_variable = {
				which = Oonoi_joins
				value = 15
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1000

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			NOT = {
				has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_langeyru_slavery
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			NOT = {
					native_policy = native_policy_coexist
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			has_any_disaster = no
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = {
				which = Oonoi_joins
				value = 1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					any_empty_neighbor_province = {
						culture = oonoi
					}
				}
				random_empty_neighbor_province = {
					limit = {
						culture = oonoi
					}
					save_event_target_as = empty_neighbor_target
				}
			}
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				is_colony = yes
			}
			save_event_target_as = first_colony_target
			set_province_flag = AD5_first_colony_flag
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				is_colony = yes
				not = {
					has_province_flag = AD5_first_colony_flag
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = second_colony_target
		}
		event_target:first_colony_target = {
			clr_province_flag = AD5_first_colony_flag
		}
	}

	option = { #They are welcome
		name = hallfredhavn.120.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		goto = empty_neighbor_target
		event_target:empty_neighbor_target = {
			create_colony = 1000
			change_culture = oonoi
			change_religion = orwaii
			random_list = {
				33 = {
					change_trade_goods = grain
				}
				33 = {
					change_trade_goods = livestock
				}
				20 = {
					change_trade_goods = fur
				}
				13 = {
					change_trade_goods = ivory
				}
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
            which = variable_AD5_hallfredhavn_food
            value = 5
		}
		add_adm_power = -20
	}

	option = { #direct them to an existing colony instead
		name = hallfredhavn.120.b
		goto = first_colony_target
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			has_saved_event_target = first_colony_target
		}
		change_variable = {
            which = variable_AD5_hallfredhavn_food
            value = 5
		}
		event_target:first_colony_target = {
			add_colonysize = 500
			add_ruinborn_minority_size_effect = yes
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "colonial_boom"
				duration = 7300
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #direct them to an existing colony instead
		name = hallfredhavn.120.c
		goto = second_colony_target
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			has_saved_event_target = second_colony_target
		}
		change_variable = {
            which = variable_AD5_hallfredhavn_food
            value = 5
		}
		event_target:second_colony_target = {
			add_colonysize = 500
			add_ruinborn_minority_size_effect = yes
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "colonial_boom"
				duration = 7300
			}
		}
	}
}

#Halfkynn dynamic growth
country_event = {
	id = hallfredhavn.135
	title = hallfredhavn.135.t
	desc = hallfredhavn.135.d
	picture = COURT_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = no
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		mission_completed = AD7_integrate_the_kynn
		any_owned_province = {
			AND = {
				culture_group = taychendi_ruinborn_elf
				OR = {
					has_human_minority_trigger = yes
					has_half_elven_minority_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				culture = halfkynn_half_elf
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #accept
		name = hallfredhavn.135.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					culture_group = taychendi_ruinborn_elf
					OR = {
						has_human_minority_trigger = yes
						has_half_elven_minority_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					culture = halfkynn_half_elf
				}
			}
			change_culture = halfkynn_half_elf
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = AD5_halfkynn_war_flag
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = AD5_halfkynn_war_modifier
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = AD5_halfkynn_trade_flag
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = AD5_halfkynn_trade_modifier
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Pay it back
country_event = {
	id = hallfredhavn.140
	title = hallfredhavn.140.t
	desc = hallfredhavn.140.d
	picture = COURT_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = no

	option = { #Pay it back now
		name = hallfredhavn.140.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = AD5_massive_loan
			}
			add_treasury = -625
			remove_country_modifier = AD5_massive_loan
			add_faction_influence = {
				faction = ad5_faction_skalir
				influence = 5
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = AD5_medium_loan
			}
			add_treasury = -312.5
			remove_country_modifier = AD5_medium_loan
			add_faction_influence = {
				faction = ad5_faction_skalir
				influence = 3
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = AD5_small_loan
			}
			add_treasury = -125
			remove_country_modifier = AD5_small_loan
			add_faction_influence = {
				faction = ad5_faction_skalir
				influence = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #I aint payin back shit
		name = hallfredhavn.140.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		add_stability = -1
		add_prestige = -25
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = AD5_massive_loan
			}
			remove_country_modifier = AD5_massive_loan
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_burghers
				loyalty = -50
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = AD5_medium_loan
			}
			remove_country_modifier = AD5_medium_loan
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_burghers
				loyalty = -25
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = AD5_small_loan
			}
			remove_country_modifier = AD5_small_loan
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_burghers
				loyalty = -10
			}
		}
	}
}

	picture = COLONIZATION_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = no
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		mission_completed = AD7_the_great_power
		any_owned_province = {
			OR = {
				culture = derannic
				culture = pearlsedger
				culture = tefori
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 365
	}

	option = { #"We will force the landowners to sell the pits to the state."
		name = hallfredhavn.141.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture = derannic
					culture = pearlsedger
					culture = tefori
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					culture = derannic
				}
				change_culture = talderannic
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					culture = pearlsedger
				}
				change_culture = perlatter
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					culture = tefori
				}
				change_culture = divenori
			}
		}
	}
}

#Stability brings prosperity
country_event = {
	id = hallfredhavn.148
	title = hallfredhavn.148.t
	desc = hallfredhavn.148.d
	picture = PEASANTS_BARTERING_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = no

	trigger = {
		has_disaster = sidrvetr
		mission_completed = AD5_diversify_food_production
		stability = 1
		NOT = {
			num_of_rebel_armies = 1
		}
		NOT = {
			num_of_rebel_controlled_provinces = 1
		}
	}

	option = { #Return
		name = hallfredhavn.148.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		change_variable = {
			which = variable_AD5_hallfredhavn_food
			value = 10
		}
		capital_scope = { add_prosperity = 50 }
		custom_tooltip = AD5_food_efficiency_buff_tt
		set_country_flag = AD5_food_efficiency_buff_flag
	}
}

#Food stuff hidden
country_event = {
	id = hallfredhavn.1000
	title = hallfredhavn.1000.t
	desc = hallfredhavn.1000.d
	picture = FAMINE_eventPicture
	goto = 2495
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { mission_completed = AD5_end_the_sidrvetr }
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = hallfredhavn.1001
				days = 1
			}
			country_event = {
				id = hallfredhavn.1000
				days = 365
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = priorStockpile
				which = variable_AD5_hallfredhavn_food
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = baseFishProduction
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = baseGrainProduction
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = livestockProduction
				value = 0
			}

			set_variable = {
				which = fishingEfficiency
				value = 0.6
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = farmingEfficiency
				value = 0.6
			}

			set_variable = {
				which = totalProduction
				value = 0
			}

			set_variable = {
				which = totalProduction
				value = 0
			}

			set_variable = {
				which = foodConsumption
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = baseSpoilage
				value = 3
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = preventableSpoilage
				value = 5
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = saltProduction
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = theftLoss
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = armyConsumption
				value = 0
			}

			set_variable = {
				which = totalLoss
				value = 0
			}

			set_variable = {
				which = totalChange
				value = 0
			}

			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = fish
				}
				export_to_variable = {
					which = baseFishProduction
					value = base_production
				}
				PREV = {
					change_variable = {
						which = baseFishProduction
						which = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = grain
				}
				export_to_variable = {
					which = baseGrainProduction
					value = base_production
				}
				PREV = {
					change_variable = {
						which = baseGrainProduction
						which = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = livestock
				}
				export_to_variable = {
					which = livestockProduction
					value = base_production
				}
				PREV = {
					change_variable = {
						which = livestockProduction
						which = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_modifier = AD5_wool_shortage
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = fishingEfficiency
					value = 0.2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_modifier = AD5_metal_shortage
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = fishingEfficiency
					value = 0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_metal_rationing
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = fishingEfficiency
					value = 0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					2301 = {
						NOT = {
							has_province_modifier = AD5_mediocre_seeds
						}
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = farmingEfficiency
					value = 0.2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_modifier = AD5_metal_shortage
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = farmingEfficiency
					value = 0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = AD5_food_efficiency_buff_flag
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = farmingEfficiency
					value = 0.2
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = fishingEfficiency
					value = 0.2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_metal_rationing
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = farmingEfficiency
					value = 0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = magic_realm_transmutation_plant_growth_1
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = farmingEfficiency
					value = 0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = magic_realm_transmutation_plant_growth_2
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = farmingEfficiency
					value = 0.2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = magic_realm_transmutation_plant_growth_3
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = farmingEfficiency
					value = 0.3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = magic_realm_transmutation_plant_growth_4
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = farmingEfficiency
					value = 0.4
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = modifiedFishProduction
				which = baseFishProduction
			}
			multiply_variable = {            
				which = modifiedFishProduction
				which = fishingEfficiency
			}
			round_variable = {
				which = modifiedFishProduction
				value = -1
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = modifiedGrainProduction
				which = baseGrainProduction
			}
			multiply_variable = {            
				which = modifiedGrainProduction
				which = farmingEfficiency
			}
			round_variable = {
				which = modifiedGrainProduction
				value = -1
			}

			change_variable = {
				which = totalProduction
				which = modifiedFishProduction
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = totalProduction
				which = modifiedGrainProduction
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = totalProduction
				which = livestockProduction
			}

			#LOSS STUFF
			export_to_variable = {
				which = foodConsumption
				value = total_development
			}
			divide_variable = {
				which = foodConsumption
				value = 3
			}
			round_variable = {
				which = foodConsumption
				value = -1
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = salt
				}
				export_to_variable = {
					which = saltProduction
					value = base_production
				}
				PREV = {
					change_variable = {
						which = saltProduction
						which = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			subtract_variable = {
				which = preventableSpoilage
				which = saltProduction
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = theftLoss
				value = average_unrest
			}
			round_variable = {
				which = theftLoss
				value = -1
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = armyConsumption
				value = army_size
			}

			change_variable = {
				which = totalLoss
				which = foodConsumption
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = totalLoss
				which = baseSpoilage
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = preventableSpoilage
						value = 0.9 #lol just to make sure 1 counts
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = totalLoss
					which = preventableSpoilage
				}
			}
			if = {
                limit = {
                    NOT = {
                        check_variable = {
                            which = theftLoss
                            value = 0
                        }
                    }
                }
                set_variable = {
                    which = theftLoss
                    value = 0
                }
            }
			change_variable = {
				which = totalLoss
				which = theftLoss
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = totalLoss
				which = armyConsumption
			}

			set_variable = {
				which = totalChange
				which = totalProduction
			}
			subtract_variable = {
				which = totalChange
				which = totalLoss
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = variable_AD5_hallfredhavn_food
				which = totalChange
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Let them do what they do best
		name = hallfredhavn.1000.a
	}
}

#Food stuff
country_event = {
	id = hallfredhavn.1001
	title = hallfredhavn.1001.t
	desc = hallfredhavn.1001.d
	picture = FAMINE_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { mission_completed = AD5_end_the_sidrvetr }
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = AD5_rampant_starvation
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = variable_AD5_hallfredhavn_food
						value = 33
					}
				}
			}
			remove_country_modifier = AD5_food_shortages
			remove_country_modifier = AD5_rationing
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = AD5_rampant_starvation
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = AD5_food_shortages
				}
				check_variable = {
					which = variable_AD5_hallfredhavn_food
					value = 33
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = variable_AD5_hallfredhavn_food
						value = 66
					}
				}
			}
			remove_country_modifier = AD5_rampant_starvation
			remove_country_modifier = AD5_rationing
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = AD5_food_shortages
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = AD5_rationing
				}
				check_variable = {
					which = variable_AD5_hallfredhavn_food
					value = 66
				}
			}
			remove_country_modifier = AD5_rampant_starvation
			remove_country_modifier = AD5_food_shortages
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = AD5_rationing
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = hallfredhavn.1001.a
		custom_tooltip = AD5_food_census_tooltip2
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = variable_AD5_hallfredhavn_food
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = hallfredhavn.4
			}
		}
	}
}
